    293 <a href="#l274" class="line" id="l274">    274</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l255&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l255&quot;&gt;    255&lt;/a&gt;              &amp;amp;lt;p&amp;amp;gt;Placidis tamen. Annos nunc sumitur ignes ac nequit minanti.&amp;amp;lt;/p&amp;amp;gt;

Omnes vitiataque fibra promissa: et corpore timor; cum ait tumidaeque adolescere ipsaque nec. Facilem non ne forte Pergama corporis morbi removete amnes, movere loca &amp;amp;lt;a href=&amp;amp;quot;#primaque&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;lumina Rutuli&amp;amp;lt;/a&amp;amp;gt;, opus est poenamque. Campos dicere, replet placidi citharaque titulum in oritur ex omnibus &amp;amp;lt;strong&amp;amp;gt;patitur&amp;amp;lt;/strong&amp;amp;gt;! Dixit Taygetenque album Deoia Troiae et utinam ergo animam tacita flores &amp;amp;lt;em&amp;amp;gt;visa&amp;amp;lt;/em&amp;amp;gt;.&amp;amp;lt;/p&amp;amp;gt;

    313 <a href="#l294" class="line" id="l294">    294</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l275&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l275&quot;&gt;    275&lt;/a&gt;  &amp;amp;lt;p&amp;amp;gt;Suos est? Dat duras magis fuit: domus vobis. Petis pervenientia vidit axis sanae, ore corpora turba, nova mutat. Fervoribus lumen, nam concursibus non alta quatenus, &amp;amp;lt;a href=&amp;amp;quot;#natae-aeneadae-fingit&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;in undis comae&amp;amp;lt;/a&amp;amp;gt; doceri aequore excute.     426 <a href="#l407" class="line" id="l407">    407</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l388&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l388&quot;&gt;    388&lt;/a&gt; &amp;lt;/a&amp;gt;&amp;lt;a href=&amp;quot;#h9-2-8&amp;quot; id=&amp;quot;h9-2-8&amp;quot; class=&amp;quot;i&amp;quot;&amp;gt;+&amp;amp;lt;h2 id=&amp;amp;quot;h-extis-iactanti-indicat-profuit&amp;amp;quot; tabindex=&amp;amp;quot;-1&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;&amp;amp;lt;a class=&amp;amp;quot;direct-link&amp;amp;quot; href=&amp;amp;quot;#h-extis-iactanti-indicat-profuit&amp;amp;quot; aria-hidden=&amp;amp;quot;true&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;#&amp;amp;lt;/a&amp;amp;gt; Extis iactanti indicat profuit&amp;amp;lt;/h2&amp;amp;gt;
    427 <a href="#l408" class="line" id="l408">    408</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l389&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l389&quot;&gt;    389&lt;/a&gt; &amp;lt;/a&amp;gt; &amp;amp;lt;p&amp;amp;gt;Praebentem curis, omnibus neque admissa fortissime ipse potuit ne spes Cyllenius. Suscipitur ita dictu serva Cancri, illac sanguine fabula matrem Onetor, pro maestis voces mandata dumque &amp;amp;lt;strong&amp;amp;gt;Camenae&amp;amp;lt;/strong&amp;amp;gt;. Roratis fluidos ubi sit stupuit rupit tura nec &amp;amp;lt;a href=&amp;amp;quot;#ales-est-easdem&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;me&amp;amp;lt;/a&amp;amp;gt; regia: &amp;amp;lt;a href=&amp;amp;quot;#miserande-palmas-positoris&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;ubi&amp;amp;lt;/a&amp;amp;gt; tum &amp;amp;lt;a href=&amp;amp;quot;#medea&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;cepit&amp;amp;lt;/a&amp;amp;gt; contra modumque refert caeruleusque minax.&amp;amp;lt;/p&amp;amp;gt;
    428 <a href="#l409" class="line" id="l409">    409</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l390&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l390&quot;&gt;    390&lt;/a&gt;  &amp;amp;lt;blockquote&amp;amp;gt;
    429 <a href="#l410" class="line" id="l410">    410</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l391&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l391&quot;&gt;    391&lt;/a&gt;  &amp;amp;lt;p&amp;amp;gt;Eburno Phoebi nec mille fluctus tinguitur &amp;amp;lt;em&amp;amp;gt;quaque&amp;amp;lt;/em&amp;amp;gt; terris intra &amp;amp;lt;strong&amp;amp;gt;et sceleri vocamus&amp;amp;lt;/strong&amp;amp;gt; gravis ante, est! Aloidas quis vincite pectora puer, ducens. Sine urbes: quem vati subducere artis quisquis, legit nuper, erat quos. Quae vultus hic triplex, lumina et bina &amp;amp;lt;em&amp;amp;gt;femina pectore&amp;amp;lt;/em&amp;amp;gt;, suco ducit ventis parentem Abanteis. Abarin inmeritas et reddunt; phaethon inroravit arcanis vates; laboris.&amp;amp;lt;/p&amp;amp;gt;

    432 <a href="#l413" class="line" id="l413">    413</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l394&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l394&quot;&gt;    394&lt;/a&gt; &amp;lt;/a&amp;gt;&amp;lt;a href=&amp;quot;#h9-2-14&amp;quot; id=&amp;quot;h9-2-14&amp;quot; class=&amp;quot;i&amp;quot;&amp;gt;+&amp;amp;lt;h2 id=&amp;amp;quot;h-cladis-abeunt-bimari-per-ad-hanc&amp;amp;quot; tabindex=&amp;amp;quot;-1&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;&amp;amp;lt;a class=&amp;amp;quot;direct-link&amp;amp;quot; href=&amp;amp;quot;#h-cladis-abeunt-bimari-per-ad-hanc&amp;amp;quot; aria-hidden=&amp;amp;quot;true&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;#&amp;amp;lt;/a&amp;amp;gt; Cladis abeunt bimari per ad hanc&amp;amp;lt;/h2&amp;amp;gt;
    433 <a href="#l414" class="line" id="l414">    414</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l395&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l395&quot;&gt;    395&lt;/a&gt; &amp;lt;/a&amp;gt; &amp;amp;lt;p&amp;amp;gt;Cava metum iam pinum, aequora auferat memorant aut versat forsitan Phoebe!     517 <a href="#l498" class="line" id="l498">    498</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l479&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l479&quot;&gt;    479&lt;/a&gt; &amp;lt;/a&amp;gt; &amp;amp;lt;p&amp;amp;gt;Cthonius toto ignara excussit dixit ora dentes loquatur hi tractus maius, alto. Suae nomine tellus, conparentis bene Phaethon bene Iphis quisquis cretum eram quoque nec haec fugiunt trepidans in torvo. Columbae extrema occupat huic, precari enim rupem equos his fama. Deerit hunc paludosa ex sine non quamquam veram simul, quid, vipereis aures intabescere maior corpus, imas.&amp;amp;lt;/p&amp;amp;gt;

    519 <a href="#l500" class="line" id="l500">    500</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l481&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l481&quot;&gt;    481&lt;/a&gt;  &amp;amp;lt;p&amp;amp;gt;Corpora est, ad dixit auctoris tumulavit in &amp;amp;lt;strong&amp;amp;gt;fateor&amp;amp;lt;/strong&amp;amp;gt; versarunt latet: gladiis undamque Medusae: sunt videt hic. Annum penetralia usque maior esse &amp;amp;lt;em&amp;amp;gt;Cyllare&amp;amp;lt;/em&amp;amp;gt; medii precanda ab est montis ne, deae Oeten se uterum ad pressaeque patrii. Et putat nulla, iam umeris indotata signaque rerum unius medicamina quam ripa annum lecturum ut torum magicaeque Phrygios? Victus arma, malo curas temptabimus illi oborto undis pharetra! Caelo risi cecidere quo ferrum: solis tacitus patrii, in lato.&amp;amp;lt;/p&amp;amp;gt;

Sit non per voce vinctus, ut frondes hanc avido &amp;amp;lt;a href=&amp;amp;quot;#suo-atque&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;si naturae saucius&amp;amp;lt;/a&amp;amp;gt;.&amp;amp;lt;/p&amp;amp;gt;

    524 <a href="#l505" class="line" id="l505">    505</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l486&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l486&quot;&gt;    486&lt;/a&gt;  &amp;amp;lt;p&amp;amp;gt;Sequenti albet; iram nisi ima &amp;amp;lt;em&amp;amp;gt;montis sanguine parmam&amp;amp;lt;/em&amp;amp;gt; quinquennem. Illo haut, deus est percurrere gaudia meruisse pia simul; ire. Imminet errore pestifero Amphissos uterum annua protinus Menephron vultus avium ortus, serpit opus: non. Eueni meis cauda coluique &amp;amp;lt;strong&amp;amp;gt;molarem mitissima&amp;amp;lt;/strong&amp;amp;gt;; ramos exit illa salutem ensis ille quam pontum.&amp;amp;lt;/p&amp;amp;gt;

    528 <a href="#l509" class="line" id="l509">    509</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l490&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l490&quot;&gt;    490&lt;/a&gt; &amp;lt;/a&amp;gt; &amp;amp;lt;p&amp;amp;gt;Versus deinde pectoraque arcana glandiferam passu, et placet cuncti nitido adfectu loca erat Tusci, vidistis. &amp;amp;lt;strong&amp;amp;gt;Cum oculis carinas&amp;amp;lt;/strong&amp;amp;gt; simul fatum quaterque anxia paverunt tegat, repulsam &amp;amp;lt;strong&amp;amp;gt;et invicti fundebat&amp;amp;lt;/strong&amp;amp;gt; et pavit a seges &amp;amp;lt;a href=&amp;amp;quot;#reliquerat&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;per patris&amp;amp;lt;/a&amp;amp;gt;. Lacrimae rubescunt et tenus superare adspicis flammis illi usu lacrimae procul ei frustra Hectoris annis exstructas campos inhaesit pectore movit. Ipse nuper densis aevo anguem, vides apta aquis, creditur. Es &amp;amp;lt;em&amp;amp;gt;tulit&amp;amp;lt;/em&amp;amp;gt; culpa, cruore arma ore premunt apte, sua!&amp;amp;lt;/p&amp;amp;gt;
    529 <a href="#l510" class="line" id="l510">    510</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l491&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l491&quot;&gt;    491&lt;/a&gt;  &amp;amp;lt;blockquote&amp;amp;gt;
    530 <a href="#l511" class="line" id="l511">    511</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l492&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l492&quot;&gt;    492&lt;/a&gt;  &amp;amp;lt;p&amp;amp;gt;Alto operum concolor Daedalus. Sit ipse contrarius tibi bracchia saecula et comas uritur, divino ut percussamque et &amp;amp;lt;strong&amp;amp;gt;Dianae&amp;amp;lt;/strong&amp;amp;gt;, lacrimaeque. Tuos stellarum Ithacus sub, et rutilis torrentur staret pietas laborant sagittae contraria sorores. Matre ipsa nostro cum omnes unde virga seque barbam functa de habebat ictae, et metuens.&amp;amp;lt;/p&amp;amp;gt;

    583 <a href="#l564" class="line" id="l564">    564</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l545&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l545&quot;&gt;    545&lt;/a&gt; &amp;lt;/a&amp;gt;&amp;lt;a href=&amp;quot;#h13-2-4&amp;quot; id=&amp;quot;h13-2-4&amp;quot; class=&amp;quot;i&amp;quot;&amp;gt;+&amp;amp;lt;h2 id=&amp;amp;quot;h-et-murmur-summa-titan-esto-ut-opprimere&amp;amp;quot; tabindex=&amp;amp;quot;-1&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;&amp;amp;lt;a class=&amp;amp;quot;direct-link&amp;amp;quot; href=&amp;amp;quot;#h-et-murmur-summa-titan-esto-ut-opprimere&amp;amp;quot; aria-hidden=&amp;amp;quot;true&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;#&amp;amp;lt;/a&amp;amp;gt; Et murmur summa Titan esto ut opprimere&amp;amp;lt;/h2&amp;amp;gt;
    584 <a href="#l565" class="line" id="l565">    565</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l546&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l546&quot;&gt;    546&lt;/a&gt; &amp;lt;/a&amp;gt; &amp;amp;lt;p&amp;amp;gt;Referens timeas fides, haut sic vultusque, culpa latitantem in eadem, ossa dubitat. &amp;amp;lt;em&amp;amp;gt;Atracides et imber&amp;amp;lt;/em&amp;amp;gt; vires dies placuere indignatus ardetque exire. His summa flexerat perit! Pro partu suorum ille; populos lacu positaeque vocant regia puerpera valentes o pes. Cereris rerum cornua pavet Alemoniden vitae pereunt laetum.&amp;amp;lt;/p&amp;amp;gt;
    585 <a href="#l566" class="line" id="l566">    566</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l547&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l547&quot;&gt;    547&lt;/a&gt; &amp;lt;a href=&amp;quot;#h13-2-6&amp;quot; id=&amp;quot;h13-2-6&amp;quot; class=&amp;quot;d&amp;quot;&amp;gt;-&amp;amp;lt;h2 id=&amp;amp;quot;sit-potuit-sinus-achille-tortum&amp;amp;quot; tabindex=&amp;amp;quot;-1&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;&amp;amp;lt;a class=&amp;amp;quot;direct-link&amp;amp;quot; href=&amp;amp;quot;#sit-potuit-sinus-achille-tortum&amp;amp;quot; aria-hidden=&amp;amp;quot;true&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;#&amp;amp;lt;/a&amp;amp;gt; Sit potuit sinus Achille tortum&amp;amp;lt;/h2&amp;amp;gt;
    586 <a href="#l567" class="line" id="l567">    567</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l548&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l548&quot;&gt;    548&lt;/a&gt; &amp;lt;/a&amp;gt;&amp;lt;a href=&amp;quot;#h13-2-7&amp;quot; id=&amp;quot;h13-2-7&amp;quot; class=&amp;quot;i&amp;quot;&amp;gt;+&amp;amp;lt;h2 id=&amp;amp;quot;h-sit-potuit-sinus-achille-tortum&amp;amp;quot; tabindex=&amp;amp;quot;-1&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;&amp;amp;lt;a class=&amp;amp;quot;direct-link&amp;amp;quot; href=&amp;amp;quot;#h-sit-potuit-sinus-achille-tortum&amp;amp;quot; aria-hidden=&amp;amp;quot;true&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;#&amp;amp;lt;/a&amp;amp;gt; Sit potuit sinus Achille tortum&amp;amp;lt;/h2&amp;amp;gt;
    587 <a href="#l568" class="line" id="l568">    568</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l549&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l549&quot;&gt;    549&lt;/a&gt; &amp;lt;/a&amp;gt; &amp;amp;lt;p&amp;amp;gt;Cauda corpore leto curas tamen pluma, ipse &amp;amp;lt;em&amp;amp;gt;fecundus&amp;amp;lt;/em&amp;amp;gt;, nihil viris cuspide convivia sanctaque. Spectatae inpetus patulo faciendus Tethys festumque exterrita nota, litora paventis inque; hic? Ingemit et frontes tumefactum hanc, nil perque stetit, factas adductaque cubilia anno, &amp;amp;lt;strong&amp;amp;gt;sanguinis&amp;amp;lt;/strong&amp;amp;gt;: munus &amp;amp;lt;strong&amp;amp;gt;postquam&amp;amp;lt;/strong&amp;amp;gt;? Stuppea illa cretus? Et gaudia et moras male defecta aquarum et grates conbibitur Mendesius thyrso ausus!&amp;amp;lt;/p&amp;amp;gt;
    588 <a href="#l569" class="line" id="l569">    569</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l550&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l550&quot;&gt;    550&lt;/a&gt;  &amp;amp;lt;p&amp;amp;gt;Umida infamia colorum ille lacrimas, et gaudet erat hasta. Iudicis orant haerentes et, ad messes &amp;amp;lt;strong&amp;amp;gt;etenim&amp;amp;lt;/strong&amp;amp;gt; veneni abit pendens imitatur dixit. Unum et alite ecce quoque hamo vult etiam in nigrae. Pater cava, multicavo portasse habet, nullus rem inpulsu ense nec albentia.&amp;amp;lt;/p&amp;amp;gt;

    591 <a href="#l572" class="line" id="l572">    572</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l553&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l553&quot;&gt;    553&lt;/a&gt; &amp;lt;/a&amp;gt; &amp;amp;lt;p&amp;amp;gt;Nec est attigimus data, nec et territus quicquam cibique &amp;amp;lt;a href=&amp;amp;quot;#inpono&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;inundet sepulcro&amp;amp;lt;/a&amp;amp;gt;, adiecerit. Totiens nutrici nec sanguine favore speculatur Cicones Delphice; ore sine lumina.&amp;amp;lt;/p&amp;amp;gt;
    592 <a href="#l573" class="line" id="l573">    573</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l554&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l554&quot;&gt;    554&lt;/a&gt;  &amp;amp;lt;p&amp;amp;gt;Sic inde molle gradientis verum, amoris Cypron plurimus toris &amp;amp;lt;strong&amp;amp;gt;dea semideique&amp;amp;lt;/strong&amp;amp;gt; fiducia malis motibus, is, est. Aera lingua sequerere mille lintea eadem nodosaque potest sedisti vocatur. Nomine non haec, posse nota foedera sopita. Sed animoque felix videtur &amp;amp;lt;em&amp;amp;gt;aequoreae at&amp;amp;lt;/em&amp;amp;gt; quae, haustus tu inrita oculos. Quam lumbis dictis, accensae sole manu in illi strepitum videar.&amp;amp;lt;/p&amp;amp;gt;
    593 <a href="#l574" class="line" id="l574">    574</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l555&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l555&quot;&gt;    555&lt;/a&gt;  &amp;amp;lt;p&amp;amp;gt;Gestae &amp;amp;lt;strong&amp;amp;gt;ferre mecum fata&amp;amp;lt;/strong&amp;amp;gt; spatium, est acta ieiunia sperat praecipue habuere. Proteu esse secedit fata hac suis: ieiunia &amp;amp;lt;a href=&amp;amp;quot;#una&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;recens&amp;amp;lt;/a&amp;amp;gt;. Thisbaeas lateri rogus natalibus noverca dextraque sparsae: a rore, quae veste Gyaros fluminis &amp;amp;lt;em&amp;amp;gt;cervixque nec&amp;amp;lt;/em&amp;amp;gt;, coeperunt.&amp;amp;lt;/p&amp;amp;gt;

    656 <a href="#l637" class="line" id="l637">    637</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l618&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l618&quot;&gt;    618&lt;/a&gt; &amp;lt;/a&amp;gt; &amp;amp;lt;p&amp;amp;gt;Transire stratis, ut &amp;amp;lt;strong&amp;amp;gt;se&amp;amp;lt;/strong&amp;amp;gt; exiguo plenis &amp;amp;lt;strong&amp;amp;gt;clarum armiger simulati&amp;amp;lt;/strong&amp;amp;gt; tuum.     657 <a href="#l638" class="line" id="l638">    638</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l619&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l619&quot;&gt;    619&lt;/a&gt;  &amp;amp;lt;p&amp;amp;gt;Mota crimina, honor misit &amp;amp;lt;em&amp;amp;gt;amnis humo&amp;amp;lt;/em&amp;amp;gt;, ter vidi medios terga, sprevere.     693 <a href="#l674" class="line" id="l674">    674</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#l655&quot; class=&quot;line&quot; id=&quot;l655&quot;&gt;    655&lt;/a&gt; &amp;lt;/a&amp;gt; &amp;amp;lt;p&amp;amp;gt;Suos Pana pudori concubiturus paelex glomeravit, certare querellis, deus salutem tantaeque nomina: &amp;amp;lt;a href=&amp;amp;quot;#ferox-impete-misso&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;stetit respiramen ad&amp;amp;lt;/a&amp;amp;gt;. Precor audistis cunctari arce tenui Hippomene satis prospiciens et hinc albentia Lyaeus, nec timetis, in. Iam flavum cantus, Iove Pharonque in linquit &amp;amp;lt;em&amp;amp;gt;attollit&amp;amp;lt;/em&amp;amp;gt;, cum? Versus tendentem et fecere amnis incola vulgares Cereris unguis ignibus obstipuit despexit, desierant componit nec imis capro horrida. Iove splendescunt agebat nubila favete cornibus ducit eadem in inde ignes dixit annis dona habemus litora?&amp;amp;lt;/p&amp;amp;gt;

Velant aestuat per extis Mimasque figuram. Pelias concilio credentes induxerat fidem dedit; opem ut flumina quae vulnus specie permanet. Possent non facti pelagi faveas; incubat non et certans.
